| 0:40:24| Consideration of a resolution of the Commission of Knox County, Tennessee, memorializing Dan York Boring.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-jan-2410-preview?start=2424)|
| 0:40:31| Do we have a motion?| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-jan-2410-preview?start=2431)|

| 0:40:34| I'll second.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-jan-2410-preview?start=2434)|
| 0:40:35| All those in favor?| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-jan-2410-preview?start=2435)|
| 0:40:36| Aye.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-jan-2410-preview?start=2436)|
| 0:40:37| Commissioner Smith and Owenby, you're recognized.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-jan-2410-preview?start=2437)|
| 0:40:40| Thank you, Mr. Chairman.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-jan-2410-preview?start=2440)|
| 0:40:41| We'll ask the family members and friends if they would like to come forward.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-jan-2410-preview?start=2441)|
| 0:40:45| We're going to let you speak, too.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-jan-2410-preview?start=2445)|
| 0:40:52| Coach, you come down here, too.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-jan-2410-preview?start=2452)|
| 0:40:59| Mr. Chairman, would you like to be read into the record, please?| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-jan-2410-preview?start=2459)|
| 0:41:03| Whereas Dan York Boring passed away on October the 11th, 2010, at the age of 90.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-jan-2410-preview?start=2463)|
| 0:41:10| Whereas Mr. Boring was born and raised and lived nearly all his life in the Fountain City community.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-jan-2410-preview?start=2470)|
| 0:41:15| Whereas Mr. Boring graduated from Central High School in 1940, where he played blocking back on the football team| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-jan-2410-preview?start=2475)|
| 0:41:21| and was a member of the undefeated 1936 and 1939 squads.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-jan-2410-preview?start=2481)|
| 0:41:28| And whereas following his high school, Dan York Boring attended the University of Chattanooga on a football scholarship,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-jan-2410-preview?start=2488)|
| 0:41:34| and in addition to playing football in Chattanooga, he proved to be a successful boxer, earning a Golden Globe Award.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-jan-2410-preview?start=2494)|
| 0:41:41| Whereas Mr. Boring's studies were interrupted by World War II when he was called to serve in the United States Army as an MP.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-jan-2410-preview?start=2501)|
| 0:41:50| Whereas after being honorably discharged from the Army in 1946, at the rank of sergeant,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-jan-2410-preview?start=2510)|
| 0:41:55| he returned to Knoxville to complete his bachelor's degree at the University of Tennessee.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-jan-2410-preview?start=2515)|
| 0:42:00| Whereas following his college graduation, Dan York Boring began his career as a coach| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-jan-2410-preview?start=2520)|
| 0:42:05| and educator at the Landon High School in Jacksonville, Florida,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-jan-2410-preview?start=2525)|
| 0:42:09| while simultaneously earning his master's degree at the University of Florida.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-jan-2410-preview?start=2529)|
| 0:42:13| And whereas in 1951, Mr. Boring returned to Knoxville and Central High School as head football coach,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-jan-2410-preview?start=2533)|
| 0:42:18| a position he held until 1957, leading the Bobcats to a 53-16-6 record during his tenure.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-jan-2410-preview?start=2538)|
| 0:42:26| And whereas Mr. Boring was named principal of Central High School in 1958| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-jan-2410-preview?start=2546)|
| 0:42:30| and commendably served in that position until his retirement in 1982,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-jan-2410-preview?start=2550)|
| 0:42:35| educating and mentoring thousands of young people during their 24 years.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-jan-2410-preview?start=2555)|
| 0:42:40| And whereas Mr. Boring had the honor of having Central High School football stadium named after him in 1982.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-jan-2410-preview?start=2560)|
| 0:42:47| And whereas after retiring as an educator, Mr. Boring served for 23 years| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-jan-2410-preview?start=2567)|
| 0:42:52| as a bailiff for the late Honorable Ray L. Jenkins of the Knox County Criminal Court.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-jan-2410-preview?start=2572)|
